(assert Engine); Constraint 3 , Source: GroupCardinality

    (and (not SRWU-Single-Wheel-Axle) SRWU-Double-Wheel-Axle))); Constraint 6 , Source: GroupCardinality

    Indicator-Lights)); Constraint 12 , Source: GroupCardinality

     (=> (not Frame-Rigid) Load-AGV_U_1_0))); Constraint 14 , Source: formula4-ActiveOperations
